2026/07/13, 8:42 am - The Network Connection: Stiaan, here is the version I would put on the table if someone gave you R1 million tomorrow.

The first thing: I would not spend it building a huge platform. That is the trap.

I would spend it proving one thing:

> Can TCN create measurable human-to-business connections at scale?



If yes, capital follows.

If no, a bigger app does not save it.


---

TCN 12-Month Execution Plan — R1 Million

Phase 1: Foundation & MVP (Month 1–2)

Budget: R250k

Objective: Build the smallest version that proves the network.

Product

Build:

User side

WhatsApp onboarding

User profile

Referral/connection identity

Opportunity feed

Notifications


Business side

Vendor registration

Business profile

Offers

Lead management


Admin

User analytics

Connection tracking

Fraud monitoring


Do NOT build yet:

❌ Native iOS app
❌ Native Android app
❌ Blockchain
❌ Complex AI matching
❌ Payments ecosystem

Those are phase 3 problems.


---

Phase 2: First Network (Month 3–5)

Budget: R300k

This is where most startups fail.

They build technology.

You build density.

Target:

Users

5,000 people

Businesses

500 businesses

Connections

10,000+ tracked interactions

Revenue

First R50k–R100k monthly revenue


---

The first vertical matters.

I would NOT launch "everything".

I would choose one.

My recommendation:

Primary:

Small business opportunity network

Why?

Because businesses have money.

Examples:

landscapers

builders

trades

consultants

service providers


A person recommends someone.

TCN records the connection.

Business gets value.

Everybody wins.


---

Phase 3: Build the moat (Month 6–9)

Budget: R250k

Now add intelligence.

Trust score

Every connection creates reputation data.

Example:

A vendor receives:

successful referrals

response speed

customer satisfaction

completed jobs


Now TCN becomes more than a directory.

It becomes a trust engine.


---

Introduce AI

Not gimmicks.

Useful AI:

"Who in this network is most likely able to help?"

Example:

A business needs: "Someone who installs irrigation systems in Johannesburg."

TCN finds:

verified suppliers

previous successful connections

trusted recommendations



---

Phase 4: Investor readiness (Month 10–12)

Budget: R200k

Now prepare the raise.

You want:

Metrics

20,000 users

2,000 businesses

50,000 connections

measurable revenue


Then you are no longer pitching an idea.

You are pitching a machine.


---

Team structure

With R1 million, I would NOT hire a big team.

I would build:

Founder/CEO

You.

Your role:

vision

partnerships

capital

network growth


Senior developer

Part-time/full-time.

Growth person

Community + partnerships.

Designer/UX

Contract.

That's enough.


---

The investor pitch

This is the sentence I would build around:

> "TCN is building the trust infrastructure for human commerce. We turn informal connections into verified economic opportunities."




---

Revenue model

Multiple layers.

Businesses

Subscription:

R199–R999/month

For:

profile

leads

analytics



---

Transactions

Small success fee.

Example:

A R50,000 job comes through TCN.

TCN receives 2%.


---

Premium trust profiles

Businesses pay for:

verification

reputation

visibility



---

The LMGI question

This is where it gets interesting.

I would not kill LMGI.

I would reposition it.

LMGI becomes:

The first human-powered growth network inside TCN.

Example:

A person introduces:

customer → plumber

plumber → supplier

supplier → builder


Everybody gets recognised.

The network grows.


---

Biggest risks

Risk 1: Founder bandwidth

Probability: HIGH

Your ideas move faster than operational execution.

Solution:

One roadmap. One dashboard. One priority.


---

Risk 2: Trying to save the world too early

Probability: HIGH

TCN could become:

jobs platform

social network

marketplace

investment platform

AI assistant


Eventually maybe.

Not now.


---

Risk 3: No network density

Probability: MEDIUM

A network with 500 random people is worthless.

A network with 500 people in one ecosystem is powerful.


---

My honest valuation view

Today:

TCN as an idea/prototype: R2m–R10m potential value

Not because of code.

Because of architecture.

After traction:

50k users + revenue:

R50m–R200m possible valuation

Large-scale African network:

R1bn+ is not impossible

But that requires years, not months.


---

The biggest thing I would tell you:

You have been acting like a developer trying to build a product.

The shift now is:

Stop building features. Start engineering a network.

Your first investor is not a VC.

Your first investor is the first 1,000 people who prove they need TCN.
